[维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告（2020年7月31日）第58期（共 966人）（二）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2020/07/202073158-966_31.html)
------

<div>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on"><br /><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">第二部分：（<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">B. <o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">巴依木拉提·那如孜别克（哈）、巴鲁宁、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白国显、白霞、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白玛益西（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">班阔吉（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">别丽花、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">包国华、包义、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鲍乃刚、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卞丽潮、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">别热克汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>朵兰汗（哈萨克）、别依力汗•萨合达提及其儿子（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">部金香、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">巴依木拉提·那如孜别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1990</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，伊宁县卡拉亚尕奇乡奥依曼布拉克村居民，职业不详，哈萨克斯坦国绿卡持有者，中国在押政治犯。巴依木拉提·那如孜别克早期曾到上海市某高中上学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又曾前往中国邻国——哈萨克共和国（又称哈萨克斯坦国，简称“哈国”），在阿拉木图市大学攻读学位，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月返回中国新疆；因其在哈国留学期间曾获取绿卡（即拥有哈国永久居住权），回国生活数载后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，突然被新疆伊宁县警方莫名抓走，送当地政治教育中心接受“再教育培训”（实则被监禁羁押）；被囚长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，因其对培训方式及内容等心存抵触，培训结果表现不佳，故不仅未被释放返家，反被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，被新疆伊宁县法院一审以不明罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">巴鲁宁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">网名“迦南”，山东烟台公民。出生在一个飞行世家，早年接受过民主启蒙，一直活跃在互联网上，微信号被封号<span lang="EN-US">7-8</span>次。最近支持香港反送中期间，巴鲁宁在各微信群中发表言论声援香港。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早<span lang="EN-US">5:00</span>钟被烟台市公安局福山分局国保支队抓捕后关押并刑事拘留。目前羁押在烟台市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白国显：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。白国显被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省绥化市北林区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，绥化市法轮功学员杨传厚、白霞、王芳、王福华、赵婷婷去兰西县北安村发送法轮功资料，被兰西县公安国保和北安镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在兰西县拘留所。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被黑龙江省安达市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白玛益西（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Pema Yeshi</span>，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）尼达村农民，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处死刑，缓期两年执行，后改判为无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">班阔吉（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，女，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县城关镇人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾在当地发生示威活动时，因政治诉求而两次遭到当局数月拘押，获释后一直处于被严密监控中。 <span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日突然再次被抓，自此失联，后得知她被指控涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛尊者八十岁寿辰活动”而遭逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，据悉当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">别丽花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省双辽市法轮功学员。别丽花女士在双辽发电厂工作，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被双辽国保大队长徐强伙同双辽公安局辽西派出所警察从工作单位抓捕，并对她住所搜查。别丽花先被关押在双辽看守所，后来又转到四平市看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">包国华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江金华圣爱堂牧师，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被金华市公安局婺城分局以涉嫌非法经营罪、聚众扰乱社会秩序罪、隐匿会计凭证罪、侵占罪四个罪名刑事拘留。被抓之前，包牧师曾拒绝金华市宗教局强制整改（实质是拆除）新教堂顶部的十字架。包国华牧师拒绝的理由是<span lang="EN-US">-----</span>新教堂的施工、规划手续齐全，不是违法建筑，不应当整改（拆除）。在被拘留后的第<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日金华日报、浙江卫视以“清廉牧师”的贪婪人生大篇幅报道包国华牧师及其妻子邢文香牧师的所谓犯罪事实。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，包国华牧师被金华市婺城区法院控告犯有“职务侵占罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“非法经营罪”以及“隐匿会计凭证、会计账簿、财务会计报告罪”等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪名，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，并处没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">包义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鲍乃刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北京山维权人士。男，湖北省京山县宋河镇人，复转军官，曾在绵阳市北川县经商，因为父上访申冤<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，被当局栽赃入监两年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因在网上响应茉莉花革命，被当局以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，后羁押于绵阳市看守所长达<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，之后被逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被取保获释送回原籍湖北。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，鲍乃刚因旁听武汉王芳涉嫌寻衅滋事案庭审遭户籍地京山县公安局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日处罚。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，鲍乃刚向京山县人民法院对京山县公安局提起行政诉状，要求撤销京山县公安局京公（宋河）行决字<span lang="EN-US">1101</span>号行政处罚决定书，责令恶意剥夺公民权利的京山县公安局向公众公开道歉。后遭法院枉法判决。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日鲍乃刚刚到北京就被湖北京山维稳人员强行劫持，押解回当地，第二天，鲍乃刚在京山公安局接受询问并被抄家，警方拿走了鲍乃刚的电脑、手机，以及一些上诉材料等。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日鲍乃刚被京山警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。现关押在京山市看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卞丽潮：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河北省人，原河北省唐山市开滦第十中学教师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。曾因信仰和修炼法轮功，而遭到中共警方长期监控；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年初，因中共当局通过监控手段得知有法轮功学员从事光盘盒生意，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，统一部署，以“大案”“要案”为目标，在河北、辽宁、山东等十数个省份集结各地国保、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”派出所警员，按照监听查获的名单，野蛮逮捕了一百多名法轮功学员，卞丽潮亦因法轮功学员身份而被河北省唐山市警方刑拘；逮捕刑拘期间，多次遭遇严刑逼供，其妻女受到严厉威胁，其家被抄，且家中做生意用的流动资金（注：其被抓走时，家中约有十几万元现金，尚未来得及存入银行）竟被警方非法侵占，并以开假单据方式诱骗其妻签字，谎称是法轮功资金，以示为“证据”；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被河北省唐山市中级法院以“信仰、修炼法轮功邪教”为罪由重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。最初在河北省保定监狱服刑，因其不堪忍受狱中酷刑折磨（注：狱方每天会派<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个狱警带着<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个犯人对其进行轮番“包夹”监控、折磨），致其心脏病等病情严重恶化，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日起转到河北省石家庄第四监狱第八监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">别热克汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>朵兰汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城地区额敏县人，塔城地区额敏县某清真寺主持，官派任命阿訇，良心犯。曾在清真寺主持工作<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，但仍因宗教信仰自由问题而被塔城地区额敏县警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年上半年拘捕，后被当局指控为：未经许可，以伊斯兰教传统方式给一对哈萨克族新婚人念尼卡，而这对婚夫妇在婚礼的第二天才正式登记领取结婚证，此举触犯了中共“其极端化”法令，于是很快被宣布逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城地区法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前具体服刑地点不详，只知他被羁押在新疆昌吉州一所用来囚禁政治犯的大监狱中。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提及其儿子：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆阿尔泰地区青河县阿热勒乡清真寺阿訇别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提，男，哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年春天被抓，至今无下落。别依力汗的儿子，因在哈国官方宗教学校学过三个月的宗教知识，也被公安带走羁押。而别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提家族，在青河县属著名的宗教家族，他的父亲、爷爷都是阿訇，在当地有极高的知名度。由于百姓对其家族的尊敬，引来当局的恐惧，故遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">部金香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信仰人士，被拘押在北京市大兴区的公安看守所。目前代理律师为刘建军律师<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">C.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡林华、蔡伟、蔡伟华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹建山、曹进兴、曹瑞平、曹三强、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柴英芝、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常军、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">车平平、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈才香、陈法庆、陈光平、陈光秀、陈桂荣、陈海水、陈海霞、陈鹤琼、陈华清、陈开奇、陈家鸿、陈建芳、陈剑雄、陈洁、陈杰人、陈静、陈金宝、陈金荣、陈玫、陈敏、陈强、陈秋实、陈全秀、陈三灵、陈淑梅、、陈树庆、陈爽、陈天茂（福建）、陈武权、陈西、陈贤忠、陈小玲、陈小燕、陈晓彬、陈晓梅、陈亚雄、陈永明、陈玉花、陈泽奇、陈兆志、陈宗、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程德亮、程淑香、程进峰、程盼云、程渊、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成浩、成卫平、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">次成加材（藏）、次成加措（藏）、次成念扎（藏）、次旺（藏）、次旺嘉措（藏）、仓央嘉措（藏）、赤列（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔德（藏）、崔兰香、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡林华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员蔡林华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1993</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省籍人，原北京某互联网公司工作人员，“端点星”网站志愿者，新闻自由捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾在中央财经大学攻读本科；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，又接续在清华大学社会学系攻读硕士学位，直至硕士毕业；大学期间，曾积极参与大学生通识教育夏令营，并在相关青少年教育活动中做义工；被捕前，曾一直是“端点星”网站的公益志愿者；因该网站自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年搭建以来，以对抗网络封锁和审查言论为己任，长期备份微信、微博等平台被删文章，其与陈枚等公益爱好者遂据此在武汉肺炎疫情爆发期间，将网站保存的大量相关疫情文章备份发于网上，以确保信息的全面性和真实性；但此举引起中共当局的强烈不满和极端恐惧；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与陈玫等人突然被北京市朝阳区警方带走，自此失联，后知已被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”等罪由执行指定居所监视居住，至今不予释放。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡伟华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，哈尔滨市法轮功学员。大学本科毕业，从事财务统计工作多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日过遭抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，蔡伟华被入黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹建山<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，职业：工人。江苏省南通市崇川区公民。家住江苏省南通市崇川区光明西村。中共官方消息称：“北京时间<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，中国江苏盐城市响水县江苏天嘉宜化工有限公司工厂厂区内发生爆炸事故。截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日<span lang="EN-US">12</span>时，事故已造成<span lang="EN-US">78</span>人死亡。共有伤员<span lang="EN-US">566</span>人，其中危重伤员<span lang="EN-US">13</span>人，重症<span lang="EN-US">66</span>人。” 随后，对这一重大灾难事故，曹建山申请江苏响水爆炸信息公开。曹建山这一公民行动竟然遭到江苏当局报复，随后南通警方竟然以涉嫌诽谤罪将其刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹进兴：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年六十七岁，唐山市农机局退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在中共当局的“敲门行动”中，他被唐山市路北区文化路派出所警察绑架。警察非法抄家持续了三个小时，家中大量私人物品被抢劫。在警察绑架过程中，曹进兴被摔伤，缝了几针。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕，在唐山市第一看守所被关押一年多，后背生了很多皮疹。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，河北唐山市路北区一审判处曹进兴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹瑞平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北辛集市马庄乡枣营村维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">30</span>年前因实行计划生育政策，曹瑞平被做结扎手术，但手术做坏了。手术后曹瑞平身体感到非常不适，妇科病增加，时时伴有小腹痛，双腿静脉曲张，导致现在小腿比大腿还粗，肿痛行走不便。向相关部门反映均无人管，自此曹瑞平走上了上访之路。由于上访时常往外跑，不幸家中两个女儿被人强奸，其中有一人是政府官员，现此官员仍在工作岗位上工作，并未得到制裁。曹瑞平丈夫在一连串灾难来临后，抑郁而终。曹瑞平于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日去天安门被带到马家楼，当天晚上无人接，自已从马家楼离开。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午到北京国家计生委和民政部投诉无果，无奈于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日连续去天安门，后被送至马家楼，最后由辛集市马庄派出所押回并刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曹瑞平被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留于石家庄市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日对曹瑞平实施逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹三强</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：祖籍湖南，曾在当地创立家庭教会，是“中国福音会”牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年汶川地震后，曾从事四川基督教爱心工作，帮助学生及地震灾民度过难关。多年前，曹三强到云南普洱从事宣教、慈善救济及兴教办学事业，并在当地创办多所学校，帮助贫困儿童入学。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，他与基督徒景如霞从缅甸佤邦（缅甸第二特区）返国时，出于便利使用了非正式方式入境中国，被边防武警拦截拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日即被当地检察院以涉嫌“偷越国境罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日该案移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日该案在孟连县法院开庭，曹三强的亲友参加了旁听。尽管曹三强的辩护人刘培福律师认为，其当事人的行为不应构成犯罪，但他仍于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被云南省孟连县法院以“偷越国境罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元人民币，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。另一位基督徒景如霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，已当庭释放。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的曹三强牧师已转到位于云南省昆明市东郊王大桥的昆明监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柴英芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柴英芝是河北省唐山市路北区人，因为在她和前夫董文奖的离婚官司中，董文奖和他表亲陈振朝联合买通异地汉沽区的法官造假判决转移资产，致柴英芝胜诉后没有分得本该分得的资产，被逼于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年开始上访。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，柴英芝与河北访民曹连生偷渡至台湾金门被抓，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被台湾移民署遣送回国，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日分别回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午，柴英芝去国家信访局上访，被唐山市路北区公安局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，之后被以同罪名逮捕。现关押于唐山市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃省白银市白银区人，是一位部队退役伤残军人，从地方兵工厂下岗，不承认其军残证，妻离儿<span lang="EN-US">5</span>岁，父也是残疾人，母体弱多病，为生存进京上访，被白银区政府公安打压非法关押多次。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被抓进看守所，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，白锒公安分局以寻衅滋事罪逮捕常军，现羁押在白银市白银区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">车平平</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：吉林法轮功学员。硕士，吉林体育学院教师。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始迫害法轮功后，车平平曾经被关进临时关押法轮功学员的戒毒所、对外挂牌叫“法制教育培训基地”的洗脑班、拘留所，又被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在吉林省女子监狱，曾四肢被固定捆绑了半个月，被关禁闭、严管、灌食，眼睛曾被两次喷辣椒水，致右眼视力模糊，视网膜脱落。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，车平平给人介绍自己修炼法轮功，被人举报而又被长春市东朝阳路派出所抓捕，非法关押在长春市第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈才香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南京六失地农民、维权公民吴娟、陈才香、伊俊秀、吴泽玉、魏玉秀、汪蔷林被指涉嫌聚众扰乱社会秩序罪，吴娟、陈才香、伊俊秀于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日羁押至今。吴泽玉、魏玉秀、汪蔷林已取保获释。六失地农民案于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在南京市建邺区法院第一法庭开庭。未判。吴娟在看守所疑受到不人道对待，被关押逾<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，头发几乎掉光，律师呼吁法院尽快将她释放。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，吴娟等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人因江心州土地被抢占，制止施工并到售楼处交涉，然后被警方拘捕。检察院认为，土地已经被征收，但他们有判决书查明事实记载未征收。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈法庆</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江环保人士。<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，农民企业家出身。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年前，他曾经和江苏省环保人士吴立红自费在“纽约时报”刊登中英文环保公益广告，敦促当时刚上任的政治局常委，兑现环保承诺。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，陈法庆被当局以“组织领导传销活动”为由，刑事拘留。家属认为，该事件与中共十九大即将召开有关。家属称，陈法庆多年来不断受到当局打压，谋生遇到很多障碍。不到<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月前，他曾向习近平寄送锦旗，要求他及各级领导善待残疾人。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈光平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">现年<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁的江西省景德镇市中级人民法院退休法官，网名：亦忱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈光平因在微博等多个平台发文质疑乐平警方办理的一宗经济案件存在警黑勾结栽赃嫁祸的情况，称江西景德镇乐平市公安局经侦大队副大队长邵长斌等人为“黑警”并向扫黑办进行了举报，结果被对方反诉诽谤并被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈光平是于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被一审判决犯诽谤罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，并被当场收监。陈光平已上诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈光秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省广水市骆店镇骆店村维权人士，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日去北京，向有关部门控告骆店派出所所长陈学炯滥用职权，为骆店村村支书张声国非法建房出售牟利鞍前马后，将其儿子殷毅抓捕拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。进京上访后，地方驻京人员给了陈光秀<span lang="EN-US">400</span>元人民币的路费，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日陈光秀到随州刚下车，即被公安以“敲诈勒索罪”刑事拘留，现羁押于随州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈桂荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连瓦房店法轮功学员陈桂荣、陈利荣姐妹俩，在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日与法轮功学员王永生配合发放真相资料时，遭恶意举报被抓捕，被瓦房店法院非法开庭并判刑，姐姐陈桂荣遭诬判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，妹妹陈利荣遭诬判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。陈桂荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈海水：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">40</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市嘉鱼县高铁镇居民，法轮功学员。因信仰、宣传法轮功而于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在家中被嘉鱼县警方抓捕。现被送进湖北省法制教育所板桥洗脑班非法关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈海霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东法轮功学员。广东雷州市白沙镇梛楠村人，后在湛江霞山区租住，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月末，在雷州市向民众发放法轮功资料的时候，被告，遭关押了几天后，获释，回到自己租住的房子。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月初，陈海霞又被警察绑架、抄家。后遭判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在血压高不适合关押的情况下，中院维持冤判，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被关押到广州女子监狱迫害。目前，陈海霞被洗脑灌输、野蛮灌食，眼睛赤红、非常憔悴，仅一个月余，其境况令家人十分担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈鹤琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川攀枝花市法轮功学员陈鹤琼，女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午十点左右，陈鹤琼在仁和区丝绸公司住宅大院家中，被四川攀枝花市仁和区公安分局、仁和派出所、土城居委会、仁和区丝绸公司配合绑架，很多人都看到两个警察一边一个分别紧紧掐住陈鹤琼的胳膊，把陈鹤琼从家里架下楼来上的警车。听说陈鹤琼在发真相资料时被便衣摄像、跟踪，现陈鹤琼在哪儿情况不详。陈鹤琼家就母子二人，在攀枝花无亲属，儿子在外地读研、还没毕业。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年曾被仁和区公法院重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈华清：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，湖北省武汉市访民陈华清、彭秀、鄢文、刘爱香、谢友枝等十余人相约来到北京上访，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日他们在北京被武汉维稳人员截访回武汉市，当晚就被分别控制在各自的辖区派出所审讯。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，访民彭秀、刘爱香被武汉警方以“寻衅滋事”为由刑事拘留，陈华清、鄢文、谢友枝等人被处以行政拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，武汉市东湖高新区访民鄢文、谢友枝、吴彩霞、陈华清等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人行政拘留期满，本应获得自由的他们，却被再次被武汉市东湖高新分局民警全部抓走，以至于他们的家属到拘留所接人都未见其人，至今这些访民仍处于失踪状态。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈开奇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">41</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，福建省莆田市人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被福建省宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，其与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨雄、庄友布、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，陈开奇被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈家鸿</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：又名陈文胆，字数真。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生于北流隆盛镇平坡村立新组。<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年容县师范毕业后在北流从教，后获北京科技进修学院律师函授班结业，中国逻辑与语言函授大学行政法专业毕业。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年分别在北流市、玉林市创办了老好人写作代理和金头脑文案写作代理服务部。后陈家鸿通过司法考试在广西百举鸣律师事务所执业，成为一名正式执业律师。源于陈家鸿长期参与维权敏感案件从而不断遭到当局的打压。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，陈家鸿律师介入了震惊网络的“广西村民罗继标在看守所离奇死亡事件”，曾遭广西警持枪围困。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，广西律协官网发布了对陈家鸿律师的“公开谴责行业处分的通报”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，陈家鸿律师被南宁市司法局行政处罚停业半年。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，广西南宁市司法局宣布解散百举鸣律师事务所，所有律师被要求转去其他律所<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，陈家鸿律师被北流市公安局、玉林市公安局联合抓捕，家中也被抄了一些卷宗和其他东西。后获知被刑事拘留。后遭批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈建芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海著名维权人士、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“曹顺利人权捍卫者纪念奖”获奖人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早晨八点上海著名维权人士、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“曹顺利人权捍卫者纪念奖”获奖人陈建芳在家中遭上海警方秘密抓捕，关押在上海市看守所。陈建芳从一位抗争土地权的农民开始，长期从事维权活动。十多年前，她家的土地被上海市政府和房屋开发商非法征收和抢占，因得不到合法合理的安置补偿，走上了上访之路捍卫自己的权益。在多年的维权与打压的磨练中，陈建芳逐渐成为当地土地征收和房屋拆迁受害者的代言人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈建芳和曹顺利女士共同接受邀请，参加当月在日内瓦举办的人权培训活动并同时观摩联合国人权理事会会议。陈建芳在广州机场被阻拦出境。在同一天，曹顺利女士在北京机场被警方拦截并被强迫失踪。警方将陈建芳带回上海并对其拘留、调查讯问、并密切监视多日。陈建芳的人权倡导活动，招来当局对她不断地打击报复，包括恐吓，殴打和任意拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈剑雄（陈进新）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因十九大维稳，民主人士袁兵、陈剑雄（陈进新）、梁一鸣<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日遭湖北赤壁警方抓捕后，均遭刑事拘留，都被关押在赤壁看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，袁兵、陈剑雄、梁一鸣被警方分别带走，警方还出动警力数人前往两人家中进行搜查，查扣物品不详。有分析指出：三人被抓捕的原因与前两天他们前往公安局及信访局讨要说法有关。而三人信访问题产生则是因为不堪当地维稳系统最近严重骚扰所致。袁兵和陈剑雄都是广东民主活动的积极参与者，梁一鸣是陈剑雄女友。因为积极参与街头民主活动，袁兵和陈剑雄等人均曾被当局判刑，两人于去年年底和今年上半年袁兵陆续释放出来。梁一鸣是陈剑雄女朋友，今年六月初因为收留朋友，被强行关闭店铺并驱赶出广东，随后和陈剑雄一起来到湖北。后<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，梁一鸣取保获释。而袁兵、陈剑雄被批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，陈剑雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都青白江区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁。在原川化集团公司青上公司上班。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年迫害法轮功后，陈洁多次被青白江区法院判刑，第一次于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，第二次于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日早上，陈洁将一本《共产主义的终极目的》发到了青白江区大弯派出所的警察手中，被该警察抓捕，在对陈洁作出十天治安拘留后，在陈洁被关押的第八天，治安拘留改为刑事拘留。第<span lang="EN-US">12</span>天左右，构陷她的案件被移送到青白江区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈杰人：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈杰人毕业于清华大学法学院，中国资深的媒体人，先后在《南方周末》、《中国青年报》、《新京报》、《人民日报》等媒体上发表了<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多篇评论文章。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年以中国青年报记者身份踢爆武汉女大学生卖淫现象，造成轰动，但却被解雇；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年作为公益时报主编，签发批评文章，触怒当局再被炒；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月因“批评政府过多”遭人民日报解除人民网江苏视窗执行总编职务。陈杰人多年来发表数千文章，希望推进新闻自由，并倡导以网络为平台的草根监督和公民表达。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，陈杰人曾在网上公开实名举报湖南邵阳市纪委书记邓广雁严重失职和渎职。随后几天，陈杰人就下落不明，与外界失联。有消息透露，湖南公安以“涉嫌敲诈勒索、非法经营”等罪名“依法办理”陈杰人。目前，陈杰人的微信公众号显示“由用户投诉并经平台审核，涉嫌违反相关法律法规，账号已被停止使用”。后获知遭湖南警方刑事拘留。湖南省桂阳县人民法院网站发布消息：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日下午，湖南省桂阳县人民法院公开开庭，对被告人陈杰人、陈伟人、刘敏寻衅滋事、敲诈勒索、非法经营、行贿一案宣告一审判决，对被告人陈杰人以寻衅滋事罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法经营罪、行贿罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">701</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯法轮功学员，佳木斯市中心医院年轻女医生。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年初被所谓的黑龙江佳木斯“<span lang="EN-US">10.28</span>专案组”警察绑架，后被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月十日被劫持往哈尔滨女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">6</span>组，遭受了非人酷刑折磨。据投诉：头三天，犯人帮教黄丽艳为了转化法轮功学员得分，她就尽其所能的折磨法轮功学员，强制陈静等法轮功学员每天坐在<span lang="EN-US">15</span>公分的小板凳上，腰挺起来身子必须坐直，双手放在膝盖上一动不能动，如稍微不直就要挨打，把陈静的腿绑起来，嘴给堵上，扇嘴巴子，连踢带打的，拳脚相加打的身上青一块紫一块的，有时拿袜子、抹布、裤衩子堵嘴。更可恶的是把衣服都给扒光了，疯狂变态的折磨，连续折磨了三个月之久，你不转化就不让你睡觉，早晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点起床，晚上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点睡觉，如果还不转化就继续延长时间。期间，有一个叫杨旭的刑事犯每天都参与迫害法轮功学员，她指使其他犯人共同对陈静进行迫害，还说用笤帚把打不会留下后遗症，有一次把陈静的脸、眼睛都打肿了，家属来接见都没有让见，她们怕他们的暴行被曝光。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈金宝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省天台县白鹤镇访民。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年陈金宝家承包的茶园及财产被白鹤镇官员强抢及拆毁，陈金宝与王小彩夫妇上访维权多年，被多次非法拘禁及殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号，因陈金宝在北京上访，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被天台县公安抓回刑拘。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈金荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南宝丰县南关镇访民，因为丈夫驾车发生交通事故后，双方亲属互殴，陈金荣的财物被抢，警方不立案处理而上访，曾因上访被检察院以敲诈勒索罪提起公诉，后因证据不足撤诉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初被南关派出所以涉嫌妨碍公务罪刑事拘留。羁押在宝丰县看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈玫：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1993</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，陕西省人，原北京市某公益机构人员，“端点星”网站公益志愿者，新闻自由捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。学生时期曾就读于中国华南农业大学，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年毕业；大学期间，曾因热心公益而多次参与为大学生筹集书籍、组织公益讲座等活动；被捕前，曾一直是“端点星”网站的公益志愿者；因该网站旨在以对抗网络封锁和审查言论为己任，服务内容以备份新闻类内容为主，所备份的文章来自国内各大主流媒体、门户网站和微信、微博等被删文章，故而为网民保留、还原了大量详实、客观、原始的文图信息；武汉管状病毒疫情爆发时，曾因该网存有疫情相关文章备份，其与蔡伟等人为了保存疫情记忆，遂发布了与疫情相关的被删敏感报导及文章备份；但此举却引发中共当局强烈不满和极端恐惧；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被北京市朝阳区警方突然带走，自此失联，后知已被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”等罪由执行指定居所监视居住，至今不予释放。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前被羁押在北京市朝阳区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁沈阳市法轮功学员。原沈阳市辽中县（现辽中区）六间房学校优秀教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午，陈敏在豪林购物中心门口给人讲法轮功遭迫害真相时，遭一便衣抓捕抄家。后被辽中区法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后陈强被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈秋实：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">生于<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年，中国黑龙江省大兴安岭地区人，公民记者、律师、演说家。现户籍所在地是山东青岛。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年毕业于黑龙江大学法学院，开始北漂生活。在北京先后从事过餐厅服务员、酒店客房服务员、演员助理、配音员、警察媒体记者、电视编导与主持人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年取得中国律师执业证书开始从事律师工作。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年任北京隆安律师事务所律师，主要执业方向为知识产权、劳动法、争议解决。中国政法大学在职研究生在读。开始参与了几十档电视与网络法律节目、综艺节目的录制。曾在中国<span lang="EN-US">70</span>所大学进行巡回演讲。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年香港反送中运动期间，曾赴香港直播报道，后受压力返回。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日与隆安律师事务所劳雇合约到期，离开律师事务所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底，毅然决然赴武汉报道疫情。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底陈秋实赴武汉采访报道疫情真实情况，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚遭中共当局强迫失踪。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日凌晨<span lang="EN-US">2:00</span>秋实妈妈发出视频，呼吁武汉的网友帮助寻找。陈秋实在武汉的安危，受到海内外的广泛关注。其直播报道中那句：“习近平在哪里，我管不着，但是武汉我陈秋实来了。”震撼海内外网路，被广泛转发。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈全秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，湖南省岳阳县人，家庭妇女，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰和宣传法轮功，而长期遭到当局的严重打压逼迫，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚被当地筻口派出所警方抓走，并遭非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，因与法轮功成员王岳来、何根良等多人参加研读法轮功书籍活动，被警方知道后又被非法抓捕，关押在岳阳看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，陈全秀等人涉邪教案被岳阳县检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，她就被岳阳县法院枉法快速冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈三灵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省界首市王集镇人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而被多次遭界首市公安局及王集镇派出所骚扰。今年以来又因宣传法轮功资料而被非法拘捕，自此失联，近期得知他已被界首市检察院批捕。现被关押在安徽省阜阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈淑梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省白山市靖宇县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生在山东，在中共人为制造的大饥荒年代，小小年纪随父母逃荒到东北。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，陈淑梅在靖宇县江边，靖宇县公安局国保大队大队长于学军等七八个人绑架，野蛮地将陈淑梅拖到家中，完全没有顾及陈淑梅双侧股骨头坏死的剧烈疼痛，在未出示警察证、没有搜查证、没有立案决定书的情况下，强行抄家，抢走陈淑梅的大量大法书籍、师父法像和手机、笔记本电脑等私人物品。后行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，陈淑梅被刑事拘留，被送到白山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，陈淑梅被吉林省白山市靖宇县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈树庆</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，浙江省富阳县人，自由撰稿人，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中国民主党全国筹委会负责人之一，人权活动家，<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学生。<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，因其多次参与民主活动，并参与联署呼吁释放包括异议人士吕耿松在内的大陆被拘捕人士，随遭到当局报复性打压，并被警方两次以“颠覆国家政权”罪由传唤；至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，终被杭州市警方以“颠覆国家政权罪”正式刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被杭州市检察院正式批捕。目前被羁押于浙江省杭州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日在杭州中院开庭，未判决。经延期与退侦后，此案于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午宣判，陈树庆被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈爽：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">23</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市温泉居民，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在深圳市龙岗区打工期间被深圳龙岗区警方非法以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘。目前被关押在深圳市龙岗区看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">约于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被深圳市龙岗区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈天茂（福建）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建晋江维权人士。现关押在福建晋江看守所。陈案缘起于其担任合同制警察期间，在一次执行公务发生车祸而致的工伤。因工伤引发被辞退，住房被分给他人，以及待遇等纠纷，多年来陈为维权，进行了多次诉讼，多次上访，多次被拘留，又被劳教，差点被判刑。直到一年多前因涉嫌为境外提供国家秘密罪被逮捕，一年多了，他坚定地认为自己无罪。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈武权：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东维权律师陈武权因守护家乡海滩被以涉寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同时被刑事拘留的还有其同村村民<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人。陈武权是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午，应当地信访部门的通知，与<span lang="EN-US">6</span>位村民一起去谈话，但他们<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人随后被以阻挠开工的名义抓走。其中<span lang="EN-US">1</span>位村民之后被放出来，其余<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被湛江市经济技术开发区公安分局刑事拘留。之前，当地官方试图在陈武权家乡所在的海域填海，而他带领家乡的村民，捍卫他们世代赖以维生的海洋。根据村民所发布的图片和申诉材料显示，随着官方开始围堰填海，原本海产丰富的海滩和红树林都遭到严重破坏，世代渔民赖以维生的螺、蚝、沙虫等海产已经消失。村民被迫出来护海。在去年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，村民的现场护海行动受到当地警方镇压。而陈武权发布的相关文件还显示，他们已经多次向有关部门反映，希望能够叫停填海工程，但官方的回复否认填海破坏环境，并认为渔民要转型谋出路在多方申诉无门之后，陈武权日前在网上发布要求游行示威的申请，很多村民已签名。陈武权之前曾代理多宗维权案，其中最为人关注的是陈光诚侄儿陈克贵案，因此多次受官方打压，并被吊销执业资格。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，广东湛江市经济技术开发区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处陈武权有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。同时被抓捕的村民陈伟梁、陈振明、陈还森、陈春霖、陈帅、陈隆群等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半有期徒刑。陈武权自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。广东人权律师陈武权于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日转往广东四会监狱（位于广东肇庆市）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈西：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日出生，贵州省贵阳市人，原名陈友才，贵州著名民主异议人士，《零八宪章》签署者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年“学潮”期间曾因组织《沙龙联谊会》，成立“贵州爱国民主联合会”声援六四，而当局被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年曾因组织“中国民主党贵州分部”，并公开要求中共平反六四而再次被捕入狱，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被贵阳市中级人民法院以“组织、领导反革命集团罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并在贵阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年出狱后，继续从事推动民主、人权和法治建设活动，并与贵州省其他自由民主异议人士共同举办“贵州首届公民国际人权研讨会”；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，陈西还与另外三名研讨会成员依法以独立候选人身份竞选地方人大代表，但时隔两月之后，贵州省民政厅竟为此颁布了《关于取缔<span lang="EN-US">"</span>贵州公民人权研讨会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>的决定》。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日第三次被警方逮捕，理由是他在境外网站发表的文章有煽动内容， 并于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前在贵州省兴义市贵州监狱服刑；据悉，其在狱中备受官方限制，既不可与外界打电话、写信，又不可会见除直系亲属之外的其他家人，且其妻每次往返<span lang="EN-US">800</span>公里探监仅准见面<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈贤忠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁高龄时被中共贵阳市南明区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，贵阳市南明区二十多名警察，在陈贤忠家里抓捕了包括陈贤忠夫妇在内的九名法轮功学员；陈贤忠家当日被抄家后，夫妇俩被抓捕到花果园派出所，第二天被送往贵阳市烂泥沟洗脑班非法关押<span lang="EN-US">12</span>天。回家后花果园派出所要求陈贤忠夫妇在半年内每天按时去派出所报到，过程中陈夫妇不断指出这是违法行为后，又改为每周一报到一次。一周后，陈夫妇再次拒绝报到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，警察上门再次将陈夫妇抓捕到花果园派出所。陈贤忠被单独审讯六、七个小时后，被转移到贵阳市南明区看守所，他的夫人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日前后，陈贤忠家人接到南明区法院下的判决通知书，陈贤忠被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈小玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建漳州维权公民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，李红花母亲庄金莲（<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）、女儿陈小玲（<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁）被漳州龙海市公安局刑事拘留。李红花（<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁）本人则在前三日的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被龙海法院以拒不履行法律文书义务的理由司法拘留十五日。后又被龙海公安刑事拘留。一家三代女性被控的罪名都是寻衅滋事，后均转为逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">被指控的所谓犯罪的事实<span lang="EN-US">:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>起诉书指控李红花、庄金莲因对拆迁补偿不满，在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月间，多次到北京中南海周边非正常上访。并多次被训诫和处罚。其中李红花被训诫<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次，庄金莲<span lang="EN-US">14</span>次，陈小玲<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次。福建漳州维权公民李红花一家三代女性被控寻衅滋事罪案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在漳州女子看守所内开庭审理，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈小燕：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，广东深圳南山、福田公安警察同时出动，非法抓捕了七位法轮功学员，分别是杨波、肖颖（杨波妻子）、豆君、朱薏、刘利军（音）、陈小燕与吴治明。其中：刘利军（音）被深圳福田公安抓捕，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天内获释。吴治明，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，被罗湖公安分局警察绑架并抄家，在罗湖看守所出现高血压，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天后回家。陈小燕，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，原被非法关押在罗湖看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在深圳市盐田区法院被非法庭审。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈晓彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈晓梅：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;
