mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，家住黑龙江省伊春市伊春区。陈晓梅因<span lang="EN-US">30</span>年未判决的案子上北京上访多次。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被伊春市公安局以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日移送伊春市法院起诉，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日退侦，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日重新起诉，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>号上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，伊春市上甘岭区法院将以敲诈勒索罪开审陈晓梅。伊春市上甘岭区检察院称：陈晓梅采取到北京非正常上访，要挟负有稳控责任单位负责人，索要公私财物，数额较大，应当以敲诈勒索罪追求其刑事责任。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈亚雄：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，湖北武穴农行买断员工、癌患者陈亚雄近期到北京敏感地方乞讨维权，遭到北京市公安局抓捕并予以刑事拘留，目前已移交湖北武穴公安局关押。陈亚雄<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月参加中国人民解放军，在陆军第一师服役，<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月参加越边境老山地区对越反击战。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月退伍在湖北武穴市农行工作，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年农行改制，拒不将陈亚雄的军龄算工龄，依照《兵役法》第六十四条明确规定，军人服役年限计算为工龄，退出现役后与所在单位工作年限累计计算。陈亚雄于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年与单位解除劳动关系，因为农行没有把陈亚雄三年军龄计算到买断时的工龄中，这样就直接影响陈亚雄买断资金少三年的工龄钱，陈亚雄因此下岗后多次向银行反映此问题要求补上三年工龄，后湖北武穴农行和黄冈市农行分别书面承认军龄的违法事实，但一直没有解决此问题，为此陈亚雄维权上访。陈亚雄<span lang="EN-US">15</span>次到北京上访，期间多次被北京市及湖北武穴市公安行政处罚、行政拘留、刑事拘留等。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈永明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：新疆轮台县第三中学校长。陈永明于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被抓，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月即以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。中共当局指控陈永明的罪状极尽荒唐，比如说陈“在公共场所（中学教师大会）发表所谓‘普世价值观’、‘民主宪政’等言论，起哄闹事，造成公共秩序严重混乱，“推号<span lang="EN-US">@crude_prude</span>关注反党分子推特帐号<span lang="EN-US">335</span>个”，手机收藏反党照片。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈玉花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、山东菏泽市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十多岁，菏泽市牡丹区商业系统退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，程盼云、李振环、陈玉花三位法轮功女学员开着电轿车下乡，在当地农村散发法轮功真相资料，在菏泽市牡丹区安兴镇被牡丹区公安局国保大队警察跟踪抓捕。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈泽奇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1963</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，山西省太原市杏花岭区人，广东省深圳市龙岗区居民，深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部经理，计算机软件专家，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。在深圳从业<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，曾任职于多家公司的软件部负责人，为人谦和儒雅，工作成绩卓越，尤其是在深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部担任经理时，曾参与过多项软件开发，且主持研发的掌上电脑“一指禅”及“蓝精灵数码词典”是当时优秀的高新技术产品；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，而遭中共深圳当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，突然被深圳市龙岗区警方从家中抓捕刑拘，并被送往深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，指控其“系法轮功组织成员”，利用掌握的专业技术，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功，属违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案在深圳市龙岗区法院正式庭审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后经深圳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈兆志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京科技大学退休教师。陈兆志<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生人，身患多种疾病，高血压，脑梗等。陈兆志被刑事拘留的时间应该在疫情期间，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日以后。其<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>账号最后更新时间是<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，最后的两条推分别是：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2/13/2020 </span>路安艾时评：中共官场大斗争，习派人马全面接管王派系体现中共内部什么信号？气化炉到底意味着什么？<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、武汉肺炎风声鹤唳！ 习近平下死令 「应收尽收」储备<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万张床位背后。陈兆志遭抓捕的具体原因目前还不清楚。去年<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午在八宝山革命公墓门前，当领导的车队来临时，北京科技大学教授陈兆志举拳高呼：打倒李鹏！李鹏是刽子手！当场被警察抓走，遭殴打，后获释。陈兆志已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被海淀区检察院批准逮捕，其涉嫌罪名由刑事拘留时的“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪”变更为“寻衅滋事罪”。委托律师<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中旬前往海淀区看守所会见了陈兆志。陈兆志的疫情言论包括“武汉病毒不是中国病毒，是中共病毒”等，他认为这是中共在对他进行政治迫害和侵害言论自由，因此拒绝在审讯笔录上签字。已被批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈宗：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州公民。<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生，住在广东省广州市番禺区。因在网上组建“冰火岛”微信群，里面有很多墙外消息，为此在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日遭到广州警方抓捕。随后被正式批捕和起诉。陈宗因组建微信群而获罪，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被广州市荔湾区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程德亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东烟台法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，程德亮和妻子唐玉兰同时从家中被烟台开发区金桥派出所警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被关进看守所，其中，程德亮被关在烟台开发区（第二）看守所，唐玉兰被关在烟台市看守所（位于福山东留公村南）。唐玉兰于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日回家，程德亮一直被非法关押在第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，检察院将此案交到开发区法院。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午两点半，在开发区法院，程德亮被非法开庭，他的律师做了无罪释放的辩护，当庭没公布结果。在被关押<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月后，程德亮遭烟台开发区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程淑香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">济南法轮功学员、女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十岁。程淑香因坚持修炼法轮功，向民众讲真相，在<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，关押于山东省女子监狱。在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被济南长清区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。书梅、程淑香是在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日分别被槐荫区公安警察有预谋抓捕的，被非法抄家，至今被关押在济南看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日济南市槐荫区法院宣判：郑书梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，程淑香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。程淑香刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程进峰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：陕西省榆林市“三赎基督”信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被执行逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被宁夏回族自治区石嘴山市中级法院二审维持一审，以组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程盼云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、山东菏泽市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十多岁，菏泽市牡丹区检察院退休干部。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，程盼云、李振环、陈玉花三位法轮功女学员开着电轿车下乡，在当地农村散发法轮功真相资料，在菏泽市牡丹区安兴镇被牡丹区公安局国保大队警察跟踪抓捕。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程渊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公益机构长沙富能负责人。资深公益人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪刑拘，后遭正式逮捕，现羁押在湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能一直通过政府信息公开的方式尝试促进政府透明度、通过规范性文件审查的方式督促各级政府部门的红头文件合法性、通过建议信和立法倡导方式促进残疾人和乙肝、艾滋携带者等群体的平等权利。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成浩、成卫平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">父子两个及母亲樊梅相都是法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日<span lang="EN-US">13</span>时，交城县公安局卫建平（警号：<span lang="EN-US">063839</span>）带领十多个警察（有特警、便衣和警察制服三种），到文水县冀周村成浩的家里，将成浩绑架，其中一个身着便衣的女子，出示了对成浩的刑事拘留书，准备非法起诉成浩，理由是成浩给国务院、山西公安厅等部门写真相信。成浩现被非法关押在交城县。成浩的父母，成卫平和樊梅相也是法轮功学员。两人于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午被太原、祁县和文水公安局绑架至今，其中成卫平被非法关押在文水拘留所，樊梅相被非法关押在离石拘留所。原定于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日对二人进行非法庭审，后不知何故取消。成浩一家三人被绑架，家里只剩弟弟一家四口（两个年幼的孩子）和还在上学的妹妹。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 170.25pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">次成加材（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，又名次成坚参，笔名“秀真”，前四川甘孜州白玉佛学院僧人，前西北民族大学中文文学专业学生，西藏知名青年藏汉双语作家，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年进入四川甘孜州白玉佛学院为僧，学习藏传佛教知识，截止<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾先后在色达五明佛学院及德格协庆寺等多个寺庙进行过深造，并在此期间勤耕不缀，于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年出版发行《雪域悲歌》、《雪域命运》等多部藏文著作；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年底还俗进入西北民族大学攻读中文文学写作专业，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年在该大学与其他同学联合创办了《新一代》藏文杂志，担任主编，同时，他还在藏人文化网开设的“秀真博客”里，用中文撰写过多篇文章，其中著名的有《丑陋的拉萨》、《那一夜》、《那些年、那些事》等等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因其多次在大学里举办各种被政府视为非法主题的讨论会，触及了当局的敏感神经，随被当局开除学籍，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月返乡后又开办了一所业余学校，向家乡青年进行免费藏汉双语教学。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，由于比如县比如乡莫阿村、孟庆村和达塘乡等地发生多处藏人示威行动，以抗议当局强行开展“爱国再教育、家家挂红旗”的政治宣讲活动，故而被警方指控在县学校学生集体抗议和民众绝食示威等事件中有“煽动分裂国家”、“破坏社会稳定”、“公开发表非法言论”之嫌，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被警方拘捕并抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又被西藏自治区高级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”和“破坏社会稳定罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">次成加措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州夏河县九甲乡人，夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。自幼即进入拉卜楞寺为僧；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因对中共当局高压严管制度的不满，甘肃省甘南州夏河县发生了大规模僧俗藏人的抗议游行，其亦参与其中；又因被当局视为带头抗议者，随在当局对抗议藏民展开大逮捕后被迫逃离；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被甘南州警方在舟曲县抓捕刑拘，并送至甘肃省安全厅看守所关押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处无期徒刑；其不服上诉，后经甘南州中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；</b>据悉，其在关押期间，曾惨遭刑讯逼供；从被捕至判刑以来，其私聘律师权、亲属探视权及到法庭旁听审判权均被拒绝；因其行为仅为以和平抗议方式来表达内心诉求，却遭司法枉法重判，故而随后又在夏河县城、拉卜楞寺院内外出现大量抗议传单。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">次成念扎（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲市比如县夏曲乡人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Geshe Tsultrim Nyendrak</span>，那曲市比如县热丹寺僧侣、经师，政治异见僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。自幼即是那曲市比如县热丹寺藏僧，后成为一名该寺庙经师（即藏族寺庙中具有权威的领读诵经者，类似于高级知识分子或高级别教授），倍受僧尼及小区藏民推崇；但自中共当局强化了对藏民争取真正意义上的民族自治，保护藏文化、民族意识及最高精神领袖（如达赖喇嘛、班禅喇嘛等活佛）认可的独立性等的极端管控，其独立思想诉求随遭严密监控和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，次成念扎曾因高度参与热丹寺僧尼和周边藏民集体抗议，公开反对中共当局长期对藏人的极权统治，要求“西藏独立”及呼吁让流亡海外的达赖喇嘛平安返乡等，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月遭赶来的大批武警残暴镇压，其所在寺庙被强关，其与多个僧尼被抓捕；后次成念扎被旋即以不知名罪由刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，并曾关押于拉萨市某看守所，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，经拉萨市中级法院二审裁决，终被秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罪名缺详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月；据悉，狱中曾遭虐待，身体健康极差，但家属申请给予救治，遭拒。目前在拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">次旺（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏索县赤多乡人，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，索县赤多乡珍达寺僧人，藏族良心犯。因关注西藏问题，被中共当局长期秘密监控，并被警方几次拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被当地警方第一次刑捕，非法关押半年后取保候审释放。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日第二次又被刑拘，当时和他一同遭捕的还有珍达寺诵经师仓央嘉措、僧人阿次和坚参。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年初左右，被中共西藏当局强行指控非法，以不知由罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 256.5pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">次旺嘉措：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Tsewang Gyatso</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，中国在押政治犯。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾， 随于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">仓央嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区那曲人，藏族僧人，那曲地区索县赤多乡珍达寺（又称直达寺）诵经师、财务主管，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因中共当局发现西藏那曲地区索县有人利用手机和微信传播所谓 “禁止材料”（如转发印有达赖喇嘛的图片、传播涉及民族尊严的歌曲及透露被封锁的地方消息等），且在围墙上喷涂“西藏独立”等字样，遂展开大规模抓捕行动；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，多名当地僧侣及村民被当局以莫须有罪名拘捕，多数人长期下落不明，仓央嘉措亦于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被当地警方从寺庙驻地抓走，后以涉嫌“与境外联系”及“煽动他人反政府”罪由刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被当局以“向外界保持联络”和“鼓励该寺年轻僧人反抗中国政府活动”等罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。目前被羁押于西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赤列（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，藏族，中国在押政治犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（注：当日是中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平抗议示威活动；但该活动立即惨遭当地警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使上百藏人被抓，多人被打死打伤；截止同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，共有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；其本人亦因积极参与抗议示威游行，很快被警方以“参与抗议示威活动”为由抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“在示威活动中实施打砸和抢夺财物”为罪由判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔德（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">又名崔成，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县查理乡夺哇村人，原查理寺僧人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔兰香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东淄博访民。崔兰香是因为一起民事案件不服法院判决上访，因为众所周知的原因她上访<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年无果。上访期间还被多次非法拘留，限制人身自由，曾被关在精神病院遭强制治疗两年多。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年她因为到中南海找中央领导诉冤被北京警方抓获，随后依照上访人员的移交程序被送到马家楼被地方政府接回，之后淄博市临淄区齐都镇派出所决定将其拘留，因其身体原因没有执行拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日崔兰香连续被淄博市临淄区公安局拘留两次期满，又被软禁在淄博市临淄区齐都镇敬老院，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午在被政府人员看押期间失联，数日后其家属收到了公安机关寄来的刑拘人员家属通知书，崔兰香已于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">13</span>时被淄博市公安局临淄分局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，羁押于淄博市看守所。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">D.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">达吾提汗•达尔古色孜（哈萨克）、达日（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">戴学林、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">旦纯（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丹增曲卡（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓光英</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、邓洪成、邓吉琼、邓术梅、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">迪克坦开（藏）、迪娜<span lang="EN-US">.</span>依根别尔德<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁国柱</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁汉忠、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁洪娟、丁家喜、丁菊英、丁灵杰、丁雪梅、丁亚军、丁岩、丁银娟、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董斌、董俊华、董美英、董瑶琼、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">豆君、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜二伟、杜贺先、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜金花、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜泽洲、杜以合、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段守珍、段学琴、段在英、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多吉扎西（藏）、多杰扎才（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">达吾提汗﹒达尔古色孜（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县人，哈萨克族，博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县牧民，人权捍卫者。自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县先后有<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多哈萨克族人（不分年龄、职业，甚至有年轻学生及政府公务员等）因“在微信群里，讨论如何移民哈萨克斯坦国”事宜被中共当局抓捕，其亦因关注移民事宜，并积极协助哈萨克村民移民哈萨克斯坦而在此次当局大抓捕中遭受迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月突然被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县警方以涉嫌“危害国家安全罪”传唤、刑拘，后很快被温泉县检察院正式批捕，被指“帮人移民到哈萨克斯坦”就是犯了严重的政治问题。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县法院一审以“危害国家安全罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。其不服，已提起上诉。据悉，羁押期间曾惨遭酷刑毒打，病危住院，但出院后仍被立即重判，其要求聘请辩护律师也被拒绝。目前被羁押于新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">达日（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他与赞查（藏）二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">戴学林</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代中期出生，籍贯不详，广西师范大学出版社《理想国》品牌营销编辑，广西师范大学出版社北京贝贝特公司营销部重要负责人，人称广西师大理想国的主页君，知名网络推手，公益活动推动者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年始，曾因利用微博做了一项“死活读不下去作品”的调查统计，从而引起网络热议，使之意识到自己可发挥更大作用，围绕“读书”做一些吸引年轻人关注力，以及既有趣又有意的公益活动；自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年起，因与他人合作在中国大陆转售多种被中共当局视为政治禁书（例如高华的著作《红太阳是怎样升起的》等）的港台书籍，随引起中共当局警觉与监视；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因与合作人张晓雄以合作营销、四六分成方式，由其负责用微信号“禁忌的游戏”（<span lang="EN-US">jinjideyouxi2014</span>）出售多项港台书籍，并由张晓雄负责入书和寄给买家，合伙销售<span lang="EN-US">1300</span>余本，后被中共当局知晓，即将销售款中的部分金额作为被抓判刑时的罪由加以指控；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，因从深圳网上书店“壹仁网”负责人杨海玲处购买港台书籍共计￥<span lang="EN-US">17</span>万余元，利用微信号“禁忌的游戏”推广，并由杨海玲直接寄给购书者，后被中共当局获悉，随将其销售额中的￥<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万余元视为“非法出版物”涉案金额；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被警方突然从北京工作地点抓走，自此失联，直至同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月家属才知其被抓确切消息；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，警方又在其合作人张晓雄南京的住处及车库中搜走拟出售的其余图书<span lang="EN-US">291</span>本书，其中<span lang="EN-US">288</span>本后来亦被警方以“非法出版物”作为指控罪由；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年初其案件被当局开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日获悉，其已在近日被中共法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">旦纯（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“洛桑丹增”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因帮助同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感），纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，并在阿坝县城洽唐中街具体实施自焚；由于当地僧人和藏人为此举行了大规模情愿示威活动，随与中共军警发生冲突；其随后即被拉萨市警方抓捕、刑拘，并被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方以涉嫌“购买汽油策划，鼓动、帮助自焚罪”执行逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在四川省马尔康县法院开庭受审，最终被该法院更换罪名，以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丹增曲卡（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区拉萨市人，又名丹曲，藏名<span lang="EN-US"> Tenzin Choedak</span>或<span lang="EN-US">Tenchoe</span>，社会工作者，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代在印度达兰萨拉的西藏儿童村完成<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年级的教育课程；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年返回西藏，在当地的欧洲非政府组织红十字会工作，并在拉萨和日喀则等多个地区推动环保工作；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因参与拉萨的和平抗议活动，被当地警方拘捕。据悉，在拘捕期间曾遭遇严刑逼供，理由是其父曾在西藏政治舞台上活跃多年，但<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年被迫离开西藏流亡印度，严刑拷打他目的是确定其抗议行动是否受到父亲的影响；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被拉萨市中级法院以“间谍罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚款人民币一万元，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓光英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆访民，被强制关押精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">23</span>点邓光英在北京市丰台区吕村被朱家坟派出所抓捕至今，邓光英的家人至今没有收到任何拘押通知。邓光英父亲还透露，地方政府的官员曾多次上门，要求在邓光英属于精神病人的材料上签字。对地方政府的无理要求，邓光英的父亲予以断然拒绝。一个没有任何精神病症状的正常人，只不过因为信访反映问题与争取自身权益，表达诉求，就属于精神病人，就要拘禁于精神病院，这就是社会主义官僚的固有思维，然而用践踏国家法律与公民人权的方式。至今未释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓洪成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，湖南省岳阳市人，网名“成主民”，微博名“湘人血性”，自由职业者，广东省深圳市龙岗区阪田街杨美东四巷<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号租住户，深圳同城聚会公民，民主宪政追求者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因邓洪成与肖兵、王威、李南海等多人在深圳市五和餐厅聚餐，席间李南海与肖兵被陌生人拍照（事后得知是国保），<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日中午，深圳市警方前往餐厅调查，手拿李南海、肖兵的照片要求工作人员指认，当天午后邓洪成与深圳维权公民肖兵、沈力、李南海、王威被警方扣押，自此失联；其侄子邓剑峰与同城聚餐公民丁岩、董凌鹏、王军及等得知消息之后前往其住处（深圳市杨美村五巷）寻找，亦遭失联；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其在江西的家属被当地派出所警察查问，且拒绝透露当邓洪成下落及具体情况；后获知，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其叔侄二人被深圳市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行指定居所监视居住，其侄子邓剑锋后被取保候审释放；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，邓洪成被深圳市检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓吉琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。邓吉琼家住重庆市渝北区，林忠英家住重庆市巴南区。由于中共在法轮功学员的身份证上做标注，法轮功学员的正常出行时时受监控、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日一早，邓吉琼与未修炼法轮功的丈夫洪代鹏，乘高铁到成都。验票时，邓吉琼的身份证提示其法轮功学员的身份，邓吉琼和丈夫遭火车站人员拦截抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，邓吉琼亲家母林忠英也被抓捕，次日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，邓吉琼的儿子、林忠英的女婿洪柳被抓捕。他们被关押一年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，邓吉琼被重庆市江北区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，洪柳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，林忠英被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，三人同时被勒索罚金。邓吉琼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓术梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。邓术梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">迪克坦开（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，甘肃省甘南州夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人。藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。次成加措、迪克坦开两位拉卜楞寺僧人因与<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在夏河县发生的大规模僧俗民众的抗议游行，随后被抓捕。次成加措被认为是带头抗议者，在当局对抗议藏人展开大逮捕后出逃，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日于舟曲县遭捕。迪克坦开也于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">迪娜<span lang="EN-US">.</span>依根别尔德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁市人，伊犁市塔城地区鹤峰县居民，哈萨克族，新疆艺术学院学生，民间知名画家，中国在押政治犯（<span lang="EN-US">CPPC</span>编号：<span lang="EN-US">00704</span>）。曾因两次造访哈萨克国，并其绘画内容主要涉猎浓郁民族特色（即纪念、弘扬哈萨克游牧民族出现过的英雄们，以及具有民族风情的哈萨克毡房和哈萨克草原等），遂于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被新疆伊犁市当局抓走，送当地某再教育营（又称集中营）接受政治学习教育；后被当地警方以不具名罪由转正式逮捕，并被新疆伊犁市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，罪名不清；据悉，其在集中营学习期间已患严重疾病，后在关押密审期间精神失常；其父多次欲探望女儿，均遭到当局拒绝，且无法获悉其实际所患疾病名称及具体所在监狱地址。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁国柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺市清原县五名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午，清原县南口前镇法轮功学员丁国柱、徐俊英、张传文及红透山矿的杨秀芳，在清原县敖家堡乡于家堡村给村民们讲法轮功时，被告发到敖家堡乡派出所。后，被清原县国保抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，辽宁抚顺市清原县法院判处丁国柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，丁国柱的妻子王海超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，张传文<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，徐俊英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，杨秀芳<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。丁国柱刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁汉忠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，山东省潍坊市昌乐县乔官镇丁家山村村民，退伍军人，抗暴维权者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年因其住宅遭强拆而引发房屋权属争议，双方未达成拆迁安置补偿协议，后其房屋虽被当局非法偷拆和强拆过两次，但因其誓死捍卫，屡次报警，并到镇县政府多次反映逼拆问题而终使家园得以保全，遂引起当地官员的极端仇视。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日其房屋被进行第三次强拆，因来势凶猛，言行蛮横恶劣，差点使其和家人被砸在屋内，随引起冲突，其全家遭暴打群殴，其头颅前部被拆迁方严重铲伤，当即血流如注，头昏眼花。其曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次报警，但警方却迟迟未到，情急之下其被迫自卫，致使<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名暴力拆迁者受伤，后经抢救无效死亡。其亦因头部伤势过重被送进医院抢救，但很快被赶来的昌乐县警方逮捕。审讯期间，惨遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日其被山东潍坊中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥权终身。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日经山东省高院二审，要求撤销一审判决，发回重审。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日再审，最终被以“故意杀人罪”改判为死缓。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，二审维持原判。目前被羁押在潍坊市昌乐县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁洪娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>丁洪娟女士<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十一岁，在大庆市萨尔图区二手手机店做保洁工作。丁洪娟女士于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被大庆市警方抓捕、抄家，被关押于大庆市看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日对丁洪娟女士批捕。丁洪娟的父母已年近八旬，父亲半身不遂，母亲也身体欠安，平日两位老人生活都很艰难，如今又为女儿遭非法拘禁牵挂忧心，盼望女儿快点回家。黑龙江省大庆市萨尔图区法轮功学员丁洪娟女士被萨尔图区开发区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并罚款三千元，丁洪娟不服违法判决，已上诉到大庆市中级法院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁家喜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京航空航天大学获得工学学士和工学硕士（飞机制造专业）。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>至<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年在沈阳航空工业总公司、北京航空工业总公司任工程师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起转为专职律师，任职于北京市多家律师事务所。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年参与设立北京市德鸿律师事务所任高级合伙人。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起积极参与推动“随迁子女就地高考”教育平权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日与许志永等人发表致习近平等中共高层领导人公开信，要求包括习近平在内的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名中国部级以上官员率先财产公示。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日丁家喜被当局以“非法集会”罪名刑事拘留，关押在北京市第三看守所。同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，公安机关将丁家喜罪名更换为“寻衅滋事”提交检察院。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日北京市检察院一分院将案件退回公安局补充侦查，控罪更换为“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，北京市海淀区法院判处丁家喜有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日丁家喜刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点左右，北京人权律师丁家喜在朋友家中被山东国保警察带走，手机等物品被查抄。所涉理由不明。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日遭正式逮捕，关押在山东省临沭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁菊英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1948</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，上海市浦东新区人，原浦东新区唐镇大丰村倪家宅<span lang="EN-US">44</span>号村民，现浦东新区川沙镇华夏东路<span lang="EN-US">2110</span>弄<span lang="EN-US">37</span>号<span lang="EN-US">101</span>室居民，维权反腐公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，曾因其全家在村中住房遭当局强拆，宅基地（面积<span lang="EN-US">1278</span>平方米）及<span lang="EN-US">4</span>亩承包地亦被政府以“征地”为名掠夺，而过低的拆迁补偿金使其根本买不起高价安置房，随被迫到北京申诉，故而屡遭地方当局无情打压；曾被上海市警方<span lang="EN-US">24</span>次送进看守所和拘留所，被关黑监狱<span lang="EN-US">400</span>多次；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因进京投诉而被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“扰乱社会秩序”罪由刑拘，期满后又被转关押黑监狱数日；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因到浦东新区塘镇信访办协商解决征地拆迁问题，而被当地警方从川沙镇华夏东路的住地以不知名罪由带走，处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因与其他维权人士共同呼吁当局释放所有在押政治犯，及为争取中国民主自由发声呼吁，而被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，中共两会召开前期，因被当局视为维稳对象及“不安定分子”，随再次被上海市浦东新区警方以不知名罪由刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被浦东新区张江地区检察院以涉嫌“扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”转正式批捕，至今未予释放。目前被羁押于浦东新区看守所（上海市浦东新区华益路<span lang="EN-US">351</span>号，邮政编码<span lang="EN-US">: 201210</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁灵杰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：《民生观察》前编辑。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日于山东淄博亲戚家中被绑架后失联。其亲戚才发现其驻地被抄家。后证实丁灵杰是因为涉及制作视频讽刺中共领导人习近平的案件而被抓捕的，丁灵杰、李学惠、刁继军三人，先后于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬及<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，分别以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪被刑拘，后被警方正式逮捕。后关押在北京石景山看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日刑满释放。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>分丁灵杰给江苏维权人士吴继新打电话说：定州市公安局的找她。后<span lang="EN-US">12</span>点零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>分吴继新给丁灵杰打电话是关机。丁灵杰被河北保定市定州市公安局从北京带走手机关机，遭强迫失踪。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。丁雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁亚军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因为房屋被强行拆迁而逐级上访，最后被迫离开家园进京维权。上访期间被打击报复行政拘留十多次，被国办出伪证劳教一次两年，被地方做假证在北京被判九个月。多年长期在北京维权，问题始终没有解决。丁亚军身体不好，有严重的心脏病，还有严重贫血等疾病，时时刻刻药不离身。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，丁亚军在永定门汽车站附近的住所被四个不明身份的人抓到一辆无牌桑塔纳车上。丁亚军被失联后，其亲属向当地警方询问，警方表示不知情，随后，其亲属依据访友提供的线索向北京市西城区西长安街派出所询问，警方告知丁亚军已被刑拘，但未明确告知关押地点。其访友猜测，这次丁亚军被刑拘可能是因为<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日她在天安门广场所作的行为艺术。目前，已经被正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁岩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓洪成、肖兵、王军、沈力、李南海（火焱）、王威、王建华、黄安阳、李江鹏等广东深圳公民<span lang="EN-US">10</span>公民遭抓捕，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日后连续遭拘捕或强迫失踪。后警方向追寻下落的邓洪成、王军家属证实其已被羁押，被指涉颠覆。后被告知指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁银娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省绍兴市越城区北海街道塘南村村民，因强拆问题从<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年开始上访，被多次拘留并劳教一年。因丁银娟在北京高院门口上访，被绍兴市北海派处所接访人员强行拉回绍兴后，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被绍兴市公安局越城区分局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日审查起诉。此案于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日于诸暨市法院开庭审理，未判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西公民，网名“南柯舟”。自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日发出消息称被警方控制在医院，被逼删除推文，此后失联至今，情况不明。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，董斌在第一时间确认泼墨女孩董瑶琼的身份，并提供其个人、家庭信息，于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被山西国保以“利用手机、电脑使用境外推特软件声援泼墨行动，扰乱公共秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，董斌在得知董瑶琼被送入精神病院后，在推特上发起了拯救董瑶琼的联署行动，于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕，山西当局以“在社交软件上发表不实言论，散布谣言，扰乱公共秩序罪”将其再次行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，董斌被正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，他被忻府区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月监禁，并被强制删除全部推文。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，董斌出狱。他顶着压力上推特，控诉在狱中曾遭受的酷刑。当局对他的严密监，派出所治安员紧盯，不许离家，他连看病就医的自由也被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，董斌在推特发文，控诉当局对他限制出境。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，董斌再在推特发文呼吁勿忘被关精神病院的董瑶琼，在新年到来之际给她写贺年信件。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，他发出的最后一条消息：“被公安政府五人以上困在医院，逼我删除全部推文”，此后一直失联。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，推特账号<span lang="EN-US"> @realNankezhou </span>显示被冻结。一直处于强迫失踪状态。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董俊华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南郸城县董俊华因孩子董景昊打疫苗致残，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初在京呼吁要求疫苗立法，后被当地警方带回刑拘。据董俊华妻子单如艳讲述，她的孩子董景昊因接种脊灰疫苗导致残疾，属于疫苗接种异常反应，现二级伤残，她和丈夫董俊华为此上访维权多年，但至今无任何说法。在多次维权无果的情况下，今年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，丈夫董俊华和疫苗受害家长一起在京呼吁要求疫苗立法。当天下午<span lang="EN-US">1</span>点多，丈夫被北京警方抓住，随后交给地方维稳人员带回，于第二天中午<span lang="EN-US">12</span>点钟左右，被当地警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，现关押在当地看守所里。<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董美英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省太仓市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，董美英被太仓<span lang="EN-US">610</span>国保警察绑架。同时被绑架的法轮功学员还有秦艳秋与陈永林。秦艳秋、董美英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董瑶琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，湖南省株洲市攸县桃水镇人，原上海房地产公司中介职员，推特名：<span lang="EN-US">feefeefly</span>，人称“泼墨女孩”，中国曾押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因用<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>在上海市海航大厦前直播其对中共独裁专制的不满，并批评当局对百姓实施洗脑逼迫，随对中共最高领导人习近平的头像泼洒墨汁，进而引起社会广泛热议；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被上海市警方抓捕，自此失联，其推特账号被人关闭；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被上海市警方送回湖南省攸县老家，并以疑有“精神病”为由被变相关押于株洲市第三医院，直至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日其父在株洲市第三医院与女儿见面之后，方知其泼墨行为已被当局定性为“攻击国家领导人”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，取保释放，并被送到湖南省攸县桃水镇母亲住处；据悉，拘押期间其备受酷刑虐待，父亲董建彪<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日与其相见时，才知其被关押在精神病院时曾被强迫吃药，获释时已完全判若两人，由原先的活泼开朗变成沉默寡言、神情紧张且有些痴呆的样子。此前董瑶琼一直被羁押于湖南省株洲市第三医院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，董瑶琼父亲董建彪发出信息，称女儿被再次关进株洲三医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">豆君：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，广东深圳南山、福田公安警察同时出动，非法抓捕了七位法轮功学员，分别是杨波、肖颖（杨波妻子）、豆君、朱薏、刘利军（音）、陈小燕与吴治明。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，杨波、肖颖、豆君被庭审，四名律师配合默契：三位律师侧重做信仰合法的无罪辩护，辩护很精彩。他们的辩护没被法官打断，但法官似乎心不在焉，没注意听。另一位律师强调办案人员的种种违法行径。豆君，六十多岁，据悉是<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年迫害发生后开始修炼法轮功的，原籍甘肃兰州市，被深圳南山公安非法抓捕抄家。尽管家里只被抄走一本大法书和一个<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等少的可怜的所谓“证据”，却被非法批捕。之后公安威胁房东，逼她儿子搬家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，杨波、肖颖、豆君被庭审，四名律师配合默契：三位律师侧重做信仰合法的无罪辩护，辩护很精彩。他们的辩护没被法官打断，但法官似乎心不在焉，没注意听。另一位律师强调办案人员的种种违法行径。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜二伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原前知名媒体人。杜二伟<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日因言获罪被太原警方传唤近<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时，期间遭受非人道对待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日夜晚在北京被国保抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日天转回太原市以寻衅滋事罪刑拘，羁押在太原第二看守所。拘留通知书的上落款日期竟然是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜贺先：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北雄县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，杜贺先被雄县公安局国保警察抓捕。后杜贺先被保定市中院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被从保定看守所转到石家庄女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜金花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10</span>时左右，浦东新区杜金花在家里做中饭，突然被上海市公安局浦东分局川沙派出所警察没有任何法律手续强制带到川沙派出所，被构陷“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，关押在浦东新区看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">杜金花原住在上海市浦东新区机场镇。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，由于上海浦东国际机场二期项目，杜金花成了受害者、被拆迁人、失地农民。杜金花上访维权<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多年来未得到安置房子和补偿。多次去北京举报控告，至今没有相关部门解决问题。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜泽洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东济南法轮功学员。战玉彩的丈夫，大学文化。因坚持修炼法轮功，遭到中共的多次迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份被公安劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在位于济南刘长山路的原济南市劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日遭到济南泉城路派出所警察抓捕，被关押到济南看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年被劳教关押在章丘的山东省第二男子劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被济南长清区公安警察跟踪抓捕。在长清区 “<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、长清区公安国保大队的操控、指示下，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月法轮功学员杜泽洲被长清区法院判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，现关押在山东省监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜以合：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省临沂市沂南县法轮功学员，杜以合<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十六岁，家住沂南县苏村镇东菜园村，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“青岛峰会”前，他从外地打工回家，沂南公安局和苏村派出所警察多次上门骚扰他的正常生活，不允许他出去打工。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日“为防止他外出打工”，警察入室抓捕了他。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被沂南法院在沂南看守所秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在山东省济南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段守珍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：武汉市青山区人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功被长期监控和受到打压迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，当其在武汉市汉口区金家墩邮局附近宣传法轮功时，遭到青山区公安分局郑珂的构陷，随被武汉市汉口区警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月其案件被转至武汉市青山区检察院。期间因证据不足，青山区检察院两次退侦，要求补充资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日其案件已转至武汉市青山区法院，至今未审待判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段学琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古赤峰市巴林左旗法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，段学琴在巴林右旗发放法轮功台历时，被巴林右旗公安警察抓捕。后被抄家。段学琴多次遭惨无人道迫害，这次出狱不到一年，又被抓捕，日前被巴林右旗法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。段学琴被关押在巴林右旗看守所期间，曾被电击，被迫害的身体非常虚弱，在十多天以前被非法庭审时她是坐着轮椅被推进法庭的。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段在英</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体;
