font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日出生，重庆市巴南区花溪街道花溪村一社村民。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年至今已有十多次遭“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”（专门迫害法轮功的非法机构）人员、国保、警察抓捕、关押、抄家、判刑、劳教等。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日因在重庆市巴南区李家沱土桥赶场日，给他人宣传法轮功内容，遂被巴南区土桥派出所警方野蛮抓捕。其家遭查抄，期间未出示任何手续。当天晚上即被以涉嫌宣传邪教罪刑拘，自此失联，家属至今未接到任何刑拘被抓等法律文书。目前被关押在重庆市巴南区看守所（重庆市市辖区巴南区巴南区巴县大道<span lang="EN-US">41</span>号）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多吉扎西（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏拉萨著名商人、民营企业家、神湖集团创办人多吉扎西于<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被不公开审判，判处无期徒刑。</b>现西藏自治区法院给多吉扎西定的罪名是“贷款诈骗罪”，然而，该案疑点是，涉案金额仅仅<span lang="EN-US">150</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，北京法律界专家论证结果是，多吉扎西无法认定犯有贷款诈骗罪，仅仅犯挪用资金罪。并建议西藏自治区法院改判有期徒刑。据了解，多吉扎西在狱中坚持不认罪，一直苦苦等待冤案平反，而多吉扎西的哥哥因多次为弟上访，已被西藏维稳部门禁止离开拉萨市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年多吉扎西的亲人已聘请北京泽博律师事务所的王飞律师为其辩护。王飞前往拉萨后，在多次请求下，终于获得监狱方面探视机会。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多杰扎才（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达塘乡央唐区<span lang="EN-US">4</span>村人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后被以涉嫌多项罪名正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被以拉萨市中级法院以“阻止政府在‘纳拉赞巴’圣上开矿”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，以“私下向他人贷款罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，以“妨碍公务罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，数罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。目前被关押在拉萨扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">E.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">F.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">樊钧益、樊梅相、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方斌、方芳、方琼官、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯宝定、冯少勇、冯小妹、冯蕴青、丰晓燕、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付常国、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付文花、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">樊钧益：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南长沙民主人士，网名铁子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四”前被刑拘，被捕原因与其网络沿路有关，樊钧益长期从事墙外信息搬运工作，将外网信息转发至由其本人创建的微信公民群及<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，群友一度达到两三千人，目前猜测当局可能担忧其“六四”有所动作而将其刑事拘留。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">樊梅相</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">樊梅相是成浩母亲、成卫平妻子，一家都是法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日<span lang="EN-US">13</span>时，交城县公安局卫建平（警号：<span lang="EN-US">063839</span>）带领十多个警察（有特警、便衣和警察制服三种），到文水县冀周村成浩的家里，将成浩绑架，其中一个身着便衣的女子，出示了对成浩的刑事拘留书，准备非法起诉成浩，理由是成浩给国务院、山西公安厅等部门写真相信。成浩现被非法关押在交城县。成浩的父母，成卫平和樊梅相也是法轮功学员。两人于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午被太原、祁县和文水公安局绑架至今，其中成卫平被非法关押在文水拘留所，樊梅相被非法关押在离石拘留所。原定于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日对二人进行非法庭审，后不知何故取消。成浩一家三人被绑架，家里只剩弟弟一家四口（两个年幼的孩子）和还在上学的妹妹。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉人，公民记者，武汉公民记者方斌被人们誉为“活着的吹哨人”，方斌因为直播武汉疫情于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日晚上被武汉警方强行入户，在没有搜查证的情况下，对其家中电脑、手机扣押。方斌<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日以手机直播的方式去了武汉几家医院，因其在五医院的几分钟时间无意发现殡仪馆运送八具尸体堆放，此视频引起海内外舆论震动。后，方斌在视频上向全世界公开宣示<span lang="EN-US">:</span>号召国人起来全民自救、推翻暴政，开展全民反抗运动。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午遭到武汉警方破门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。方芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方琼官：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省陆良县板桥镇马长湖办事处七社维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年因曲陆高速建设，需要修建一条来回运土的临时道路，方琼官家的住房被强拆，宅基地被占，方琼官一家为此走上了<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年的上访维权之路。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，方琼官的丈夫汪海生刚到省巡视组驻陆良办公点陆良县同乐大酒店递交材料，就被当地某些人员连拖带打抬上车导致昏倒两次。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，方琼官在国家信访门口被几个大汉拖上车带走，从此长达<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天家属无法与方琼官取得联系。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日零晨<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点左右接方琼官打电话，告知这段时间被软禁，深夜将其被丢在半路。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，陆良县公安局以“解决你家的事”为由将方琼官骗走后秘密关押，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月没有通知家属。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日家属才收到陆良县公安局于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日做出的对方琼官的“寻衅滋事罪”逮捕通知书，目前方琼官被羁押在陆良县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点开庭审判后至今未下判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯宝定：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省昆明市安宁市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，冯宝定因在“昆钢”（昆明钢铁控股有限公司）粘贴“法轮大法好”标语，被中共抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被昆明市西山区法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，冯宝定在安宁市看守所收到判决，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并勒索罚金一千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯少勇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> 1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北省仙桃市张沟镇人，北京邮电大学博士，前北京邮电大学，广东省深圳市龙岗区长住居民，原深圳市某中学员工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾在北京邮电大学读博士生，为人乐观谦和，人缘好，因是研究项目组技术骨干，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在该校与同事成功研发机顶盒，并将个人所获奖金<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万全部捐给该校；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，遭中共北京当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被深圳市龙岗区警方突然抓捕，次日被刑事拘留，并被送深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其所在中学办公室、宿舍，其家及亲戚家当天均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，控其与另一法轮功友人陈泽奇“均系法轮功组织成员，二人利用掌握的专业知识，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功”，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案件被深圳市龙岗区法院开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日经深圳市中级人民法院终审裁定，驳回上诉、维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯小妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏无锡市滨湖区拆迁受害者冯小妹，因被起诉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日再次被无锡市滨湖区人民法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在无锡市第二看守所。冯小妹因房屋拆迁和家中财物被抢等问题，在当地始终无法解决，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日到北京天安门裸奔维权，被当地公安人员带回后以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。在被非法羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被无锡市公安局滨湖分局批准逮捕，在关押期间，冯小妹被两次强迫做精神病鉴定，其家人多次前往交涉无果，之后因为滨湖区雪浪街道要跟冯小妹谈拆迁问题，于是在今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日将她取保候审释放回家。在取保期间，冯小妹并未进京上访维权，却于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又被滨湖区法院以同样罪名批准逮捕关押。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯蕴青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉法轮功学员。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被绑架，关押在武汉东西湖区武汉第一看守所。参与绑架和扣押的部门有：武汉市网监支队，武汉市“国保”支队，江岸区公安分局后湖派出所。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冯蕴青不服判决，上诉到武汉市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月武汉中级法院二审维持原判。现在冯蕴青被非法关押在武汉女子监狱（位于武汉市宝丰路）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丰晓燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">毕业于山东师范大学新闻系，临沂市人大副调研员，副县级。二十多年公职期间因不满现有体制不被提拔，不允出国，不准考取研究生博士职称学历，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被市政府组织黑社会撞断腰，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年春天退党退公职，单位拒绝。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月公开支持香港反送中，被送进派出所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年新冠疫情间对体制内失察渎职，捐款贪污，罔顾人命，胡作非为忍无可忍，故上京发声。却被侮辱为精神病并强制治疗。丰晓燕拒不认罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被送至临沂第四精神病院，北京路育才路派出所二十多位警察，将患有腰椎间盘突出的丰晓燕在水泥地板拖行至住院部三楼，未进行精神检测，强行关进精神病医院。污蔑其为精神分裂症并强制用药。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付常国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“佳士事件”被捕人士，<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>组织<span lang="EN-US">-</span>深圳打工者中心工作人员。据悉，付常国的姐姐付红娥于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日向深圳市坪山区公安分局递交“取保候审申请书”，深圳警方否决申请并认为“付常国可能毁灭、伪造证据，干扰证人作证或者串供，采取取保候审不足以阻止发生社会危害性”，因此不予变更强制措施。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付文花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省南漳县武安镇人，因为<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月她儿子付学刚遭遇车祸后对方不承担医疗费，交警不予处理让他到法院起诉而上访，上访期间被对此殴打、拘留<span lang="EN-US">,</span>曾在拘留所被迫割腕自尽。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花在京被南漳县武安镇派出所强行押回后被拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，关押在南漳拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午武安镇政府李才明书记和几个不明身份人员强行将付文花从南漳拘留所抬出来塞进车里带走，进行私自拘禁、酷刑虐待并讹诈，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花被折磨至昏死而丢在路旁被人救起。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，付文花被南漳县公安局抓走，关押在湖北省南漳县看守所。付文花于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点在南漳县法院秘密开庭，被以寻衅滋事罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><br /></div>
</div>
